daoyu_state_modifier_remove_global_variable_effect = {
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_state_negative_birth_rate_mult
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_state_positive_birth_rate_mult
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_growth_mortality
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_migration_pull
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_state_assimilation_mult
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_decree_road_maintenance
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_decree_promote_social_mobility
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_throughput_and_input_mult
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_decree_enlistment_efforts
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_building_minimum_wage_mult
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options
	every_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } remove_variable = daoyu_state_modifier }
}

daoyu_create_character = {
	if = {
		limit = { is_ai = no }
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = daoyu_create_general }
			create_character = { age = 20 is_general = yes ig_leader = no noble = no interest_group = $IG$ traits = { daoyu_target_character wrathful } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_variable = daoyu_create_admiral }
			create_character = { age = 20 is_admiral = yes ig_leader = no noble = no interest_group = $IG$ traits = { daoyu_target_character wrathful } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_variable = daoyu_create_politician }
			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_noble } create_character = { age = 35 ig_leader = yes noble = yes interest_group = $IG$ traits = { daoyu_target_character } } }
			else = { create_character = { age = 35 ig_leader = yes noble = no interest_group = $IG$ traits = { daoyu_target_character } } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_variable = daoyu_create_agitator }
			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_noble } create_character = { age = 35 is_agitator = yes noble = yes interest_group = $IG$ traits = { daoyu_target_character } } }
			else = { create_character = { age = 35 is_agitator = yes noble = no interest_group = $IG$ traits = { daoyu_target_character } } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_variable = daoyu_create_ruler }
			every_scope_character = { limit = { or = { is_ruler = yes is_heir = yes } } kill_character = yes }
			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_noble } create_character = { age = 35 ruler = yes  ig_leader = yes noble = yes interest_group = $IG$ traits = { daoyu_target_character } } }
			else = { create_character = { age = 35 ruler = yes ig_leader = yes noble = no interest_group = $IG$ traits = { daoyu_target_character } } }
		}
		random_scope_character = { limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_character }
	}
	remove_variable = daoyu_noble
}
daoyu_change_target_character_culture = {
	if = {
		limit = { not = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character } }
		random_character = { limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_character }
	}
	set_global_variable = daoyu_change_target_character_culture
	daoyu_all_culture_effect = yes
}
daoyu_unit_count_effect = {
	set_variable = { name = daoyu_unit_count_var value = 0 }
	daoyu_num_collection = yes
}
daoyu_unit_count_clean_effect = {
	set_variable = daoyu_unit_count_clean
	daoyu_num_collection = yes
	remove_variable = daoyu_unit_count_clean
	remove_variable = daoyu_unit_count_var
}
daoyu_single_num = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_variable = daoyu_unit_count_clean has_variable = daoyu_unit_count_$NUM$ }
		remove_variable = daoyu_unit_count_$NUM$
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_variable = daoyu_unit_count_var }
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_filter_fleet any_military_formation = { owner = root percent > 0 filter = { is_fleet = yes } any_combat_unit = { count = $NUM$ } } }
			change_variable = { name = daoyu_unit_count_var add = 1 }
			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_01 var:daoyu_unit_count_var <= 19 } set_variable = daoyu_unit_count_$NUM$ }
			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_02 var:daoyu_unit_count_var > 19 var:daoyu_unit_count_var <= 37 } set_variable = daoyu_unit_count_$NUM$ }
			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_03 var:daoyu_unit_count_var > 37 var:daoyu_unit_count_var <= 55 } set_variable = daoyu_unit_count_$NUM$ }
			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_04 var:daoyu_unit_count_var > 55 var:daoyu_unit_count_var <= 73 } set_variable = daoyu_unit_count_$NUM$ }
			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_05 var:daoyu_unit_count_var > 73 } set_variable = daoyu_unit_count_$NUM$ }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_filter_army any_military_formation = { owner = root percent > 0 filter = { is_army = yes } any_combat_unit = { count = $NUM$ } } }
			change_variable = { name = daoyu_unit_count_var add = 1 }
			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_01 var:daoyu_unit_count_var <= 19 } set_variable = daoyu_unit_count_$NUM$ }
			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_02 var:daoyu_unit_count_var > 19 var:daoyu_unit_count_var <= 37 } set_variable = daoyu_unit_count_$NUM$ }
			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_03 var:daoyu_unit_count_var > 37 var:daoyu_unit_count_var <= 55 } set_variable = daoyu_unit_count_$NUM$ }
			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_04 var:daoyu_unit_count_var > 55 var:daoyu_unit_count_var <= 73 } set_variable = daoyu_unit_count_$NUM$ }
			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_05 var:daoyu_unit_count_var > 73 } set_variable = daoyu_unit_count_$NUM$ }
		}
	}
}

daoyu_coe = {
	random_military_formation = {
		limit = { any_combat_unit = { count = $NUM$ } }
		save_scope_as = daoyu_mf_1
	}
	random_military_formation = {
		limit = { exists = scope:daoyu_mf_1 not = { this = scope:daoyu_mf_1 } any_combat_unit = { count = $NUM$ } }
		save_scope_as = daoyu_mf_2
	}
	random_military_formation = {
		limit = { exists = scope:daoyu_mf_2 nor = { this = scope:daoyu_mf_1 this = scope:daoyu_mf_2 } any_combat_unit = { count = $NUM$ } }
		save_scope_as = daoyu_mf_3
	}
	random_military_formation = {
		limit = { exists = scope:daoyu_mf_3 nor = { this = scope:daoyu_mf_1 this = scope:daoyu_mf_2 this = scope:daoyu_mf_3 } any_combat_unit = { count = $NUM$ } }
		save_scope_as = daoyu_mf_4
	}
	random_military_formation = {
		limit = { exists = scope:daoyu_mf_4 nor = { this = scope:daoyu_mf_1 this = scope:daoyu_mf_2 this = scope:daoyu_mf_3 this = scope:daoyu_mf_4 } any_combat_unit = { count = $NUM$ } }
		save_scope_as = daoyu_mf_5
	}
	random_military_formation = {
		limit = { exists = scope:daoyu_mf_5 nor = { this = scope:daoyu_mf_1 this = scope:daoyu_mf_2 this = scope:daoyu_mf_3 this = scope:daoyu_mf_4 this = scope:daoyu_mf_5 } any_combat_unit = { count = $NUM$ } }
		save_scope_as = daoyu_mf_6
	}
	random_military_formation = {
		limit = { exists = scope:daoyu_mf_6 nor = { this = scope:daoyu_mf_1 this = scope:daoyu_mf_2 this = scope:daoyu_mf_3 this = scope:daoyu_mf_4 this = scope:daoyu_mf_5 this = scope:daoyu_mf_6 } any_combat_unit = { count = $NUM$ } }
		save_scope_as = daoyu_mf_7
	}
	random_military_formation = {
		limit = { exists = scope:daoyu_mf_7 nor = { this = scope:daoyu_mf_1 this = scope:daoyu_mf_2 this = scope:daoyu_mf_3 this = scope:daoyu_mf_4 this = scope:daoyu_mf_5 this = scope:daoyu_mf_6 this = scope:daoyu_mf_7 } any_combat_unit = { count = $NUM$ } }
		save_scope_as = daoyu_mf_8

daoyu_A_R_S_T = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_add_building_state_trait has_global_variable = daoyu_S_T_$STATE_TRAIT$ not = { has_state_trait = $STATE_TRAIT$ } }
		state_region = { add_state_trait = $STATE_TRAIT$ }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait has_global_variable = daoyu_S_T_$STATE_TRAIT$ has_state_trait = $STATE_TRAIT$ }
		state_region = { remove_state_trait = $STATE_TRAIT$ }
	}
}

	daoyu_other_S_T = { STATE_TRAIT = "building_arms_industry" }
	daoyu_other_S_T = { STATE_TRAIT = "building_chemical_plants" }
	daoyu_other_S_T = { STATE_TRAIT = "building_synthetics_plants" }
	daoyu_other_S_T = { STATE_TRAIT = "building_steel_mills" }
	daoyu_other_S_T = { STATE_TRAIT = "building_motor_industry" }
	daoyu_other_S_T = { STATE_TRAIT = "building_war_machine_industry" }
	daoyu_other_S_T = { STATE_TRAIT = "building_electrics_industry" }
	daoyu_other_S_T = { STATE_TRAIT = "building_munition_plants" }
	daoyu_other_S_T = { STATE_TRAIT = "building_power_plant" }
}
daoyu_check_add_potential_target = {
	set_global_variable = daoyu_check_add_potential_target
	daoyu_other_building_state_trait_effect = yes
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_check_add_potential_target
}
daoyu_check_remove_potential_target = {
	set_global_variable = daoyu_check_remove_potential_target
	daoyu_other_building_state_trait_effect = yes
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_check_remove_potential_target
}
daoyu_remove_all_building_state_trait = {
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait
	set_global_variable = daoyu_remove_all_building_state_trait
	daoyu_other_building_state_trait_effect = yes
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_remove_all_building_state_trait
}
daoyu_remove_building_state_trait_var = {
	set_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait_var
	daoyu_other_building_state_trait_effect = yes
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait_var
}
daoyu_one_building_one_region_effect = {
	set_global_variable = daoyu_one_building_one_region_effect
	daoyu_other_building_state_trait_effect = yes
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_one_building_one_region_effect
}
daoyu_other_S_T = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_building_one_region_effect any_scope_state = { has_state_trait = $STATE_TRAIT$ } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_building = $STATE_TRAIT$ not  = { has_state_trait = $STATE_TRAIT$ } } remove_building = $STATE_TRAIT$ }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_check_add_potential_target has_global_variable = daoyu_add_building_state_trait has_global_variable = daoyu_S_T_$STATE_TRAIT$ }
		if = { limit = { any_state = { has_state_trait = $STATE_TRAIT$ } } every_state = { limit = { has_state_trait = $STATE_TRAIT$ } remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_check_remove_potential_target has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait has_global_variable = daoyu_S_T_$STATE_TRAIT$ }
		if = { limit = { any_state = { has_state_trait = $STATE_TRAIT$ } } every_state = { limit = { has_state_trait = $STATE_TRAIT$ } set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_all_building_state_trait }
		if = { limit = { any_state = { has_state_trait = $STATE_TRAIT$ } } every_state = { limit = { has_state_trait = $STATE_TRAIT$ } state_region = { remove_state_trait = $STATE_TRAIT$ } } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait_var } remove_global_variable = daoyu_S_T_$STATE_TRAIT$ }
}

daoyu_clean_building_level_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_scope_state = {
				or = {
					has_variable = daoyu_building_coal_mine
					has_variable = daoyu_building_iron_mine
					has_variable = daoyu_building_lead_mine
					has_variable = daoyu_building_sulfur_mine
					has_variable = daoyu_building_gold_mine

dcc_created_effect = {
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = dcc_law_chiefdom not = { has_law = law_type:law_chiefdom } } activate_law = law_type:law_chiefdom }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = dcc_law_monarchy not = { has_law = law_type:law_monarchy } } activate_law = law_type:law_monarchy }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = dcc_law_presidential_republic not = { has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic } } activate_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = dcc_law_parliamentary_republic not = { has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic } } activate_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = dcc_law_theocracy not = { has_law = law_type:law_theocracy } } activate_law = law_type:law_theocracy }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = dcc_law_council_republic not = { has_law = law_type:law_council_republic } } activate_law = law_type:law_council_republic }
	remove_global_variable = dcc_law_chiefdom
	remove_global_variable = dcc_law_monarchy
	remove_global_variable = dcc_law_presidential_republic
	remove_global_variable = dcc_law_parliamentary_republic
	remove_global_variable = dcc_law_theocracy
	remove_global_variable = dcc_law_council_republic
	set_variable = dcc_country
}
dcc_create_country_or_change_tag_effect = {
	remove_daoyu_sort_global_variable = yes
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = dcc }
		remove_global_variable = dcc
		create_country = { tag = $TAG$ origin = root state = scope:dcc_capital on_created = { dcc_created_effect = yes } }
		every_state = { limit = { has_variable = dcc_capital } remove_variable = dcc_capital }
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = dcc_country } remove_variable = dcc_country save_scope_as = dcc_country }
		if = { limit = { exists = scope:dcc_country exists = scope:daoyu_tst_1 } scope:daoyu_tst_1 = { set_state_owner = scope:dcc_country } }
		if = { limit = { exists = scope:dcc_country exists = scope:daoyu_tst_2 } scope:daoyu_tst_2 = { set_state_owner = scope:dcc_country } }
		if = { limit = { exists = scope:dcc_country exists = scope:daoyu_tst_3 } scope:daoyu_tst_3 = { set_state_owner = scope:dcc_country } }
		if = { limit = { exists = scope:dcc_country exists = scope:daoyu_tst_4 } scope:daoyu_tst_4 = { set_state_owner = scope:dcc_country } }
		if = { limit = { exists = scope:dcc_country exists = scope:daoyu_tst_5 } scope:daoyu_tst_5 = { set_state_owner = scope:dcc_country } }
		if = { limit = { exists = scope:dcc_country exists = scope:daoyu_tst_6 } scope:daoyu_tst_6 = { set_state_owner = scope:dcc_country } }
		if = { limit = { exists = scope:dcc_country exists = scope:daoyu_tst_7 } scope:daoyu_tst_7 = { set_state_owner = scope:dcc_country } }
		if = { limit = { exists = scope:dcc_country exists = scope:daoyu_tst_8 } scope:daoyu_tst_8 = { set_state_owner = scope:dcc_country } }
		if = { limit = { exists = scope:dcc_country exists = scope:daoyu_tst_9 } scope:daoyu_tst_9 = { set_state_owner = scope:dcc_country } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = dcc_owned } remove_variable = dcc_owned set_state_owner = scope:dcc_country }
		if = { limit = { exists = scope:dcc_country } scope:dcc_country = { every_scope_state = { set_state_type = incorporated } } }
		clear_saved_scope = dcc_capital
		clear_saved_scope = dcc_country
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_tst_1
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_tst_2
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_tst_3
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_tst_4

		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_tst_7
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_tst_8
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_tst_9
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_become_a_nonexistent_country }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_become_a_nonexistent_country
		change_tag = $TAG$
	}
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_sort_by_chinese
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_sort_by_english
	trigger_event = { id = dcc.10 popup = yes }
}
daoyu_cultural_obsession_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_add_cultural_obsession }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = {
			every_scope_culture = { limit = { is_primary_culture_of = scope:daoyu_target_country not = { has_cultural_obsession = $GOODS$ } } hidden_effect = { add_cultural_obsession = $GOODS$ } }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_cultural_obsession }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = {
			every_scope_culture = { limit = { is_primary_culture_of = scope:daoyu_target_country has_cultural_obsession = $GOODS$ } hidden_effect = { remove_cultural_obsession = $GOODS$ } }
		}
	}
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_add_banned_goods } scope:daoyu_target_country = { limit = { not = { is_banning_goods = g:$GOODS$ } } add_banned_goods = g:$GOODS$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_banned_goods } scope:daoyu_target_country = { limit = { is_banning_goods = g:$GOODS$ } remove_banned_goods = g:$GOODS$ } }
}

daoyu_production_method_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_scope_state = { any_scope_building = { is_building_type = $TYPE$ has_active_production_method = $PM$ } }
			any_scope_state = { not = { any_scope_building = { is_building_type = $TYPE$ has_active_production_method = $PM$ } } }
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = { any_scope_building = { is_building_type = $TYPE$ not = { has_active_production_method = $PM$ } } }
			activate_production_method = { building_type = $TYPE$ production_method = $PM$ }
		}
	}
}
daoyu_auto_production_method_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_scope_state = { any_scope_building = { is_building_type = building_urban_center has_active_production_method = pm_arcades } }
			any_scope_state = { not = { any_scope_building = { is_building_type = building_urban_center has_active_production_method = pm_arcades } } }
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = { any_scope_building = { is_building_type = building_urban_center not = { has_active_production_method = pm_arcades } } }
			activate_production_method = { building_type = building_urban_center production_method = pm_arcades }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_scope_state = { any_scope_building = { is_building_type = building_urban_center has_active_production_method = pm_covered_markets } }

daoyu_single_create_country_effect = {
	set_variable = daoyu_original_country
	if = {
		limit = { any_scope_state = { count > 1 } any_scope_state = { state_region = s:$STATE$ } not = { exists = c:$TAG$ } }
		random_scope_state = { limit = { state_region = s:$STATE$ } save_scope_as = daoyu_capital }
		create_country = { origin = prev tag = $TAG$ state = scope:daoyu_capital on_created = { set_variable = daoyu_new_country } }
	}
}

daoyu_r_a_c_cu_effect = {
	scope:daoyu_target_country = {
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_r_cu } remove_primary_culture = cu:$CULTURE$ }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_a_cu } add_primary_culture = cu:$CULTURE$ }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu } every_scope_state = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { has_pop_culture = $CULTURE$ } change_pop_culture = { value = 1 target = scope:daoyu_t_cu } } } }
	}
}
daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_target_country_convert_population }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = {
			if = { limit = { not = { country_has_state_religion = rel:$RELIGION$ } } set_state_religion = rel:$RELIGION$ }
			every_scope_state = { limit = { any_scope_pop = { not = { religion = rel:$RELIGION$ } } } convert_population = { value = 1 target = rel:$RELIGION$ } }
			every_scope_character = { limit = { not = { religion = rel:$RELIGION$ } } change_character_religion = rel:$RELIGION$ }
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = { limit = { not = { country_has_state_religion = rel:$RELIGION$ } } set_state_religion = rel:$RELIGION$ }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { any_scope_pop = { not = { religion = rel:$RELIGION$ } } } convert_population = { value = 1 target = rel:$RELIGION$ } }
		every_scope_character = { limit = { not = { religion = rel:$RELIGION$ } } change_character_religion = rel:$RELIGION$ }
	}
}
daoyu_auto_religious_enforced_effect = {
	set_global_variable = daoyu_auto_religious_enforced_effect
	daoyu_religious_effect = yes
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_auto_religious_enforced_effect
}

daoyu_move_pop_religion_unemployed_effect = {
	set_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_religion_unemployed_effect
	daoyu_religious_effect = yes
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_665 } scope:daoyu_migration_from = { random_scope_pop = { limit = { culture = { has_variable = daoyu_target_culture } is_employed = no } move_pop = scope:daoyu_migration_go_to } } }
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_religion_unemployed_effect
}
daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = {
	set_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect
	daoyu_religious_effect = yes
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect
}
daoyu_single_religious_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_auto_religious_enforced_effect }
		if = {
			limit = { country_has_state_religion = rel:$RELIGION$ }
			every_scope_state = { limit = { any_scope_pop = { not = { religion = rel:$RELIGION$ } } } convert_population = { value = 1 target = rel:$RELIGION$ } }
			every_scope_character = { limit = { not = { religion = rel:$RELIGION$ } } change_character_religion = rel:$RELIGION$ }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion }
		if = {
			limit = { any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion country_has_state_religion = rel:$RELIGION$ } }
			set_state_religion = rel:$RELIGION$
			every_scope_character = { change_character_religion = rel:$RELIGION$ }
			every_scope_state = { convert_population = { value = 1 target = rel:$RELIGION$ } }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_religion_unemployed_effect }
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_$RELIGION$ }
			scope:daoyu_migration_from = { random_scope_pop = { limit = { culture = { has_variable = daoyu_target_culture } religion = rel:_$RELIGION$ is_employed = no } move_pop = scope:daoyu_migration_go_to } }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect }
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_$RELIGION$ culture = { has_variable = daoyu_target_culture } religion = rel:$RELIGION$ is_pop_type = slaves }
			change_poptype = pop_type:laborers move_pop = scope:daoyu_migration_go_to
		}
	}
}
daoyu_move_pop_religion_effect = {
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_catholic } scope:daoyu_migration_from = { random_scope_pop = { limit = { culture = { has_variable = daoyu_target_culture } religion = rel:catholic is_pop_type = $TYPE$ } move_pop = scope:daoyu_migration_go_to } } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_protestant } scope:daoyu_migration_from = { random_scope_pop = { limit = { culture = { has_variable = daoyu_target_culture } religion = rel:protestant is_pop_type = $TYPE$ } move_pop = scope:daoyu_migration_go_to } } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_orthodox } scope:daoyu_migration_from = { random_scope_pop = { limit = { culture = { has_variable = daoyu_target_culture } religion = rel:orthodox is_pop_type = $TYPE$ } move_pop = scope:daoyu_migration_go_to } } }

	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_sunni } scope:daoyu_migration_from = { random_scope_pop = { limit = { culture = { has_variable = daoyu_target_culture } religion = rel:sunni is_pop_type = $TYPE$ } move_pop = scope:daoyu_migration_go_to } } }

	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_gelugpa } scope:daoyu_migration_from = { random_scope_pop = { limit = { culture = { has_variable = daoyu_target_culture } religion = rel:gelugpa is_pop_type = $TYPE$ } move_pop = scope:daoyu_migration_go_to } } }	
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_confucian } scope:daoyu_migration_from = { random_scope_pop = { limit = { culture = { has_variable = daoyu_target_culture } religion = rel:confucian is_pop_type = $TYPE$ } move_pop = scope:daoyu_migration_go_to } } }

	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_hindu } scope:daoyu_migration_from = { random_scope_pop = { limit = { culture = { has_variable = daoyu_target_culture } religion = rel:hindu is_pop_type = $TYPE$ } move_pop = scope:daoyu_migration_go_to } } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_shinto } scope:daoyu_migration_from = { random_scope_pop = { limit = { culture = { has_variable = daoyu_target_culture } religion = rel:shinto is_pop_type = $TYPE$ } move_pop = scope:daoyu_migration_go_to } } }

daoyu_auto_single_expand_building_effcet = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_building_one_region_on }
				and = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_building_one_region_on root = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_state_trait = $BUILDING$ } } } }
				and = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_building_one_region_on has_state_trait = $BUILDING$ }
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { any_scope_building = { or = { weekly_profit > 1000 is_subsidized = yes } cash_reserves_ratio > 0.8 is_building_type = $BUILDING$ is_under_construction = no level < 2 } } create_building = { building = $BUILDING$ level = 2 reserves = 1 } }
		else_if = { limit = { any_scope_building = { or = { weekly_profit > 1000 is_subsidized = yes } cash_reserves_ratio > 0.8 is_building_type = $BUILDING$ is_under_construction = no level < 3 } } create_building = { building = $BUILDING$ level = 3 reserves = 1 } }
		else_if = { limit = { any_scope_building = { or = { weekly_profit > 1000 is_subsidized = yes } cash_reserves_ratio > 0.8 is_building_type = $BUILDING$ is_under_construction = no level < 4 } } create_building = { building = $BUILDING$ level = 4 reserves = 1 } }
		else_if = { limit = { any_scope_building = { or = { weekly_profit > 1000 is_subsidized = yes } cash_reserves_ratio > 0.8 is_building_type = $BUILDING$ is_under_construction = no level < 5 } } create_building = { building = $BUILDING$ level = 5 reserves = 1 } }

		else_if = { limit = { any_scope_building = { or = { weekly_profit > 1000 is_subsidized = yes } cash_reserves_ratio > 0.8 is_building_type = $BUILDING$ is_under_construction = no level < 9900 } } create_building = { building = $BUILDING$ level = 9900 reserves = 1 } }
		else_if = { limit = { any_scope_building = { or = { weekly_profit > 1000 is_subsidized = yes } cash_reserves_ratio > 0.8 is_building_type = $BUILDING$ is_under_construction = no level < 9950 } } create_building = { building = $BUILDING$ level = 9950 reserves = 1 } }
		else_if = { limit = { any_scope_building = { or = { weekly_profit > 1000 is_subsidized = yes } cash_reserves_ratio > 0.8 is_building_type = $BUILDING$ is_under_construction = no level < 10000 } } create_building = { building = $BUILDING$ level = 10000 reserves = 1 } }
	}
}

daoyu_auto_single_expand_building_government_administration_effcet = {

daoyu_auto_expand_building_government_administration_effcet = {
	if = {
		limit = { any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = yes is_homeland_of_country_cultures = root any_scope_building = { is_building_type = building_government_administration level < 10 } } }
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = { is_incorporated = yes is_homeland_of_country_cultures = root any_scope_building = { is_building_type = building_government_administration level < 10 } }
			daoyu_auto_single_expand_building_government_administration_effcet = yes
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = yes is_homeland_of_country_cultures = root not = { any_scope_building = { is_building_type = building_government_administration level < 10 } } }
			any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = yes not = {is_homeland_of_country_cultures = root } any_scope_building = { is_building_type = building_government_administration level < 10 } }
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = { is_incorporated = yes not = {is_homeland_of_country_cultures = root } any_scope_building = { is_building_type = building_government_administration level < 10 } }
			daoyu_auto_single_expand_building_government_administration_effcet = yes
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = yes is_homeland_of_country_cultures = root any_scope_building = { is_building_type = building_government_administration level < 20 } } }

			any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = yes not = {is_homeland_of_country_cultures = root } any_scope_building = { is_building_type = building_government_administration level < 30 } }

daoyu_auto_unemployed_effcet = {
	every_scope_state = {
		limit = { any_scope_pop = { is_employed = yes } }
		every_scope_pop = {
			limit = { is_employed = no }
			change_pop_culture = { value = 1 target = cu:daoyu_nonexistent }
		}
	}
	kill_population_percent = {
		percent = 1
		culture = cu:daoyu_nonexistent
	}
}
daoyu_auto_single_trade_route_effcet = {
	if = {
		limit = { any_country = { leading_producer_of = g:$GOODS$ } }
		if = {
			limit = { or = { has_law = law_type:law_protectionism has_law = law_type:law_mercantilism } }
			if = { limit = { any_market = { owner = root mg:$GOODS$ = { market_goods_pricier > 0.25 } } } set_tariffs_import_priority = g:$GOODS$ }
			else_if = { limit = { any_market = { owner = root mg:$GOODS$ = { market_goods_cheaper > 0.25 } } } set_tariffs_export_priority = g:$GOODS$ }
			else_if = { limit = { any_market = { owner = root mg:$GOODS$ = { market_goods_pricier <= 0.1 market_goods_cheaper <= 0.1 } } } set_tariffs_no_priority = g:$GOODS$ }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { any_market = { owner = root mg:$GOODS$ = { market_goods_pricier > 0.25 } } }
			if = { limit = { any_market = { mg:$GOODS$ = { market_goods_production >= 10 market_goods_cheaper > 0.75 } daoyu_can_create_trade_route_trigger = yes } } random_market = { limit = { mg:$GOODS$ = { market_goods_production >= 10 market_goods_cheaper > 0.75 } daoyu_can_create_trade_route_trigger = yes } owner = { create_trade_route = { goods = $GOODS$ level = 10 direction = export target = root.market } } } }
			else_if = { limit = { any_market = { mg:$GOODS$ = { market_goods_production >= 10 market_goods_cheaper > 0.7 } daoyu_can_create_trade_route_trigger = yes } } random_market = { limit = { mg:$GOODS$ = { market_goods_production >= 10 market_goods_cheaper > 0.7 } daoyu_can_create_trade_route_trigger = yes } owner = { create_trade_route = { goods = $GOODS$ level = 10 direction = export target = root.market } } } }
			else_if = { limit = { any_market = { mg:$GOODS$ = { market_goods_production >= 10 market_goods_cheaper > 0.65 } daoyu_can_create_trade_route_trigger = yes } } random_market = { limit = { mg:$GOODS$ = { market_goods_production >= 10 market_goods_cheaper > 0.65 } daoyu_can_create_trade_route_trigger = yes } owner = { create_trade_route = { goods = $GOODS$ level = 10 direction = export target = root.market } } } }
			else_if = { limit = { any_market = { mg:$GOODS$ = { market_goods_production >= 10 market_goods_cheaper > 0.6 } daoyu_can_create_trade_route_trigger = yes } } random_market = { limit = { mg:$GOODS$ = { market_goods_production >= 10 market_goods_cheaper > 0.6 } daoyu_can_create_trade_route_trigger = yes } owner = { create_trade_route = { goods = $GOODS$ level = 10 direction = export target = root.market } } } }
			else_if = { limit = { any_market = { mg:$GOODS$ = { market_goods_production >= 10 market_goods_cheaper > 0.55 } daoyu_can_create_trade_route_trigger = yes } } random_market = { limit = { mg:$GOODS$ = { market_goods_production >= 10 market_goods_cheaper > 0.55 } daoyu_can_create_trade_route_trigger = yes } owner = { create_trade_route = { goods = $GOODS$ level = 10 direction = export target = root.market } } } }

daoyu_change_ideology_same_ruler = {
	if = { limit = { ruler = { has_ideology = ideology:$IDE$ } } every_scope_character = { limit = { not = { has_ideology = ideology:$IDE$ } } set_ideology = ideology:$IDE$ } }
}

	daoyu_single_culture_effect = { CULTURE = "sulista" }
	daoyu_single_culture_effect = { CULTURE = "nordestino" }
	daoyu_single_culture_effect = { CULTURE = "amazonic" }
	daoyu_single_culture_effect = { CULTURE = "paulista" }
	daoyu_single_culture_effect = { CULTURE = "peruvian" }
	daoyu_single_culture_effect = { CULTURE = "bolivian" }
	daoyu_single_culture_effect = { CULTURE = "ecuadorian" }
	daoyu_single_culture_effect = { CULTURE = "chilean" }
	daoyu_single_culture_effect = { CULTURE = "argentine" }
	daoyu_single_culture_effect = { CULTURE = "uruguayan" }
	daoyu_single_culture_effect = { CULTURE = "venezuelan" }
	daoyu_single_culture_effect = { CULTURE = "paraguayan" }
	daoyu_single_culture_effect = { CULTURE = "colombian" }
}
daoyu_single_culture_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_add_radicals_in_state_effect }
		if = { limit = { owner = { country_has_primary_culture = cu:$CULTURE$ } state_region = { is_homeland = cu:$CULTURE$ } any_scope_pop = { strata = poor } } add_radicals_in_state = { value = 1 strata = poor } order_by = turmoil }
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { not = { country_has_primary_culture = cu:$CULTURE$ } } state_region = { is_homeland = cu:$CULTURE$ } any_scope_pop = { culture = cu:$CULTURE$ } }
			add_radicals_in_state = { value = 1 culture = cu:$CULTURE$ } order_by = turmoil 
			if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_country_add_radicals } add_culture_standard_of_living_modifier = { culture = cu:$CULTURE$ months = 1 multiplier = -10 } }
			else = { add_culture_standard_of_living_modifier = { culture = cu:$CULTURE$ months = 12 multiplier = -10 } }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_primary_culture_count_effect }
		if = {
			limit = { country_has_primary_culture = cu:$CULTURE$ }
			scope:daoyu_target_country = { change_variable = { name = daoyu_primary_culture_count add = 1 } }
			if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu } cu:$CULTURE$ = { save_scope_as = daoyu_t_cu } }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_add_homeland_for_mark_target_culture_effect }
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = dculo_$CULTURE$ }
			every_state = {
				limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_state state_region = { not = { is_homeland = cu:$CULTURE$ } } }
				state_region = { add_homeland = cu:$CULTURE$ }
				if = { limit = { not = { has_cultural_community = cu:$CULTURE$ } } add_cultural_community = cu:$CULTURE$ }
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_add_owner_homeland_remove_others_effect }
		if = {
			limit = { this = c:CHI }
			if = { limit = { state_region = { is_homeland = cu:$CULTURE$ } state_region = { remove_homeland = cu:$CULTURE$ } } }
		}
		else = {
			if = { limit = { owner = { country_has_primary_culture = cu:$CULTURE$ } } owner = { every_scope_state = { state_region = { add_homeland = cu:$CULTURE$ } } } }
			else_if = { limit = { state_region = { is_homeland = cu:$CULTURE$ } owner = { not = { country_has_primary_culture = cu:$CULTURE$ } } } state_region = { remove_homeland = cu:$CULTURE$ } }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect }
		if = { limit = { owner = { country_has_primary_culture = cu:$CULTURE$ } } state_region = { add_homeland = cu:$CULTURE$ } every_scope_pop = { change_pop_culture = { value = 1 target = cu:$CULTURE$ } } }
		else = { state_region = { remove_homeland = cu:$CULTURE$ } }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_create_pop_for_mark_target_culture_effect }
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = dculo_$CULTURE$ }
			every_state = {
				limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_state }
				daoyu_create_pop_effect = { CULTURE = $CULTURE$ }
				if = { limit = { not = { has_cultural_community = cu:$CULTURE$ } } add_cultural_community = cu:$CULTURE$ }
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_create_primary_culture_pops_effect }
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state }
			if = {
				limit = { root = { country_has_primary_culture = cu:$CULTURE$ } }
				daoyu_create_pop_effect = { CULTURE = $CULTURE$ }
				if = { limit = { not = { has_cultural_community = cu:$CULTURE$ } } add_cultural_community = cu:$CULTURE$ }
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = dculo_remove_global_variable_effect }
		remove_global_variable = dculo_$CULTURE$
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_save_mark_target_culture_effect }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = dculo_$CULTURE$ } cu:$CULTURE$ = { save_scope_as = daoyu_mark_target_culture } }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_all_primary_culture_effect }
		remove_primary_culture = cu:$CULTURE$
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_change_target_character_culture exists = scope:daoyu_target_character }
		if = {
			limit = { country_has_primary_culture = cu:$CULTURE$ }
			scope:daoyu_target_character = { change_character_culture = cu:$CULTURE$ }
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_change_target_character_culture
			clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_character
		}
	}
}
daoyu_create_pop_W_A_R = {
	create_pop = { size = $SIZE$ literacy_rate = $L_R$ working_adult_ratio = $W_A_R$ pop_type = peasants culture = $CULTURE$ }
}
daoyu_create_pop_L_R = {
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_W_A_R_04 } daoyu_create_pop_W_A_R = { SIZE = $SIZE$ L_R = $L_R$ W_A_R = "0.4" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_W_A_R_06 } daoyu_create_pop_W_A_R = { SIZE = $SIZE$ L_R = $L_R$ W_A_R = "0.6" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_W_A_R_08 } daoyu_create_pop_W_A_R = { SIZE = $SIZE$ L_R = $L_R$ W_A_R = "0.8" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_W_A_R_10 } daoyu_create_pop_W_A_R = { SIZE = $SIZE$ L_R = $L_R$ W_A_R = "1.0" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
}
daoyu_create_pop_SIZE = {
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_L_R_02 } daoyu_create_pop_L_R = { SIZE = $SIZE$ L_R = "0.2" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_L_R_04 } daoyu_create_pop_L_R = { SIZE = $SIZE$ L_R = "0.4" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_L_R_06 } daoyu_create_pop_L_R = { SIZE = $SIZE$ L_R = "0.6" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_L_R_08 } daoyu_create_pop_L_R = { SIZE = $SIZE$ L_R = "0.8" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_L_R_10 } daoyu_create_pop_L_R = { SIZE = $SIZE$ L_R = "1.0" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
}
daoyu_create_pop_effect = {
	daoyu_set_pop_default_parameters = yes
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_1K } daoyu_create_pop_SIZE = { SIZE = "1000" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_2K } daoyu_create_pop_SIZE = { SIZE = "2000" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_5K } daoyu_create_pop_SIZE = { SIZE = "5000" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_10K } daoyu_create_pop_SIZE = { SIZE = "20000" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_20K } daoyu_create_pop_SIZE = { SIZE = "20000" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_50K } daoyu_create_pop_SIZE = { SIZE = "50000" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_100K } daoyu_create_pop_SIZE = { SIZE = "100000" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_1M } daoyu_create_pop_SIZE = { SIZE = "1000000" CULTURE = $CULTURE$ } }
}
daoyu_set_pop_default_parameters = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			nor = {
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_1K
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_2K
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_5K
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_10K
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_20K
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_50K
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_100K
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_1M
			}
		}
		set_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_10K
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			nor = {
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_L_R_02
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_L_R_04
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_L_R_06
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_L_R_08
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_L_R_10
			}
		}
		set_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_L_R_10
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			nor = {
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_W_A_R_04
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_W_A_R_06
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_W_A_R_08
				has_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_W_A_R_10
			}
		}
		set_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_W_A_R_10
	}
}

	remove_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_20K

	remove_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_100K
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_set_create_pops_1M
}

daoyu_select_mtc = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_new_culture_for_name }
		cu:$CULTURE$ = { save_scope_as = daoyu_new_culture_for_name }
		trigger_event = { id = daoyu.271 popup = yes }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion }
		cu:$CULTURE$ = { save_scope_as = daoyu_only_one_culture }
		trigger_event = { id = daoyu.520 popup = yes }
	}
	else = { set_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture set_global_variable = dculo_$CULTURE$ trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
}
daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion_effect = {
	daoyu_religious_effect = yes
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_country_one_nation_one_religion } remove_global_variable = daoyu_one_country_one_nation_one_religion }
	daoyu_remove_all_primary_culture_effect = yes
	add_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_only_one_culture
	every_scope_character = { change_character_culture = scope:daoyu_only_one_culture }
	every_scope_state = {
		every_scope_pop = { if = { limit = { pop_has_primary_culture = no } change_pop_culture = { value = 1 target = scope:daoyu_only_one_culture } } }
	}
	set_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion
	if = {
		limit = { any_country = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion } } }
		random_country = { limit = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion } } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.509 days = 1 } }
	}
	else = {
		every_state = {
			every_scope_pop = { if = { limit = { pop_has_primary_culture = no } change_pop_culture = { value = 1 target = scope:daoyu_only_one_culture } } }
		}
		every_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion } remove_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion
	}
}
daoyu_remove_all_primary_culture_effect = {
	set_global_variable = daoyu_remove_all_primary_culture_effect
	daoyu_all_culture_effect = yes
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_remove_all_primary_culture_effect
}
daoyu_add_radicals_in_state_effect = {
	set_global_variable = daoyu_add_radicals_in_state_effect
	daoyu_all_culture_effect = yes
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_add_radicals_in_state_effect
}
daoyu_single_primary_culture_count_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { country_has_primary_culture = cu:$CULTURE$ }
		change_variable = { name = daoyu_primary_culture_count add = 1 }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu } cu:$CULTURE$ = { save_scope_as = daoyu_t_cu } }
	}
}
daoyu_primary_culture_count_effect = {
	set_global_variable = daoyu_primary_culture_count_effect
	scope:daoyu_target_country = {
		set_variable = { name = daoyu_primary_culture_count value = 0 }
		daoyu_all_culture_effect = yes
	}
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_primary_culture_count_effect
}
daoyu_create_primary_culture_pops_effect = {
	set_global_variable = daoyu_create_primary_culture_pops_effect
	daoyu_all_culture_effect = yes
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_create_primary_culture_pops_effect
}
daoyu_create_pop_for_mark_target_culture_effect = {
	set_global_variable = daoyu_create_pop_for_mark_target_culture_effect
	daoyu_all_culture_effect = yes
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_create_pop_for_mark_target_culture_effect
}
daoyu_add_homeland_for_mark_target_culture_effect = {
	set_global_variable = daoyu_add_homeland_for_mark_target_culture_effect
	daoyu_all_culture_effect = yes
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_add_homeland_for_mark_target_culture_effect
}
daoyu_add_owner_homeland_remove_others_effect = {
	set_global_variable = daoyu_add_owner_homeland_remove_others_effect
	every_scope_state = {
		limit = { or = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state owner = { has_variable = daoyu_all_owner_homeland } } }
		daoyu_all_culture_effect = yes
		if = { limit = { owner = c:CHI state_region = { not = { is_homeland = cu:han } } } state_region = { add_homeland = cu:han } }
	}
	remove_variable = daoyu_all_owner_homeland
	remove_global_variable = daoyu_add_owner_homeland_remove_others_effect
}
daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect = {
	scope:daoyu_target_country = { religion = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_religion } }
	if = {
		limit = { this = c:CHI }
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = { or = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state owner = { has_variable = daoyu_all_owner_homeland } } }
			every_scope_pop = { limit = { not = { culture = cu:han } } change_pop_culture = { value = 1 target = cu:han } }
			convert_population = { value = 1 target = scope:daoyu_target_religion }
		}
		daoyu_add_owner_homeland_remove_others_effect = yes
	}
	else = {
		set_global_variable = daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = { or = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state and = { is_incorporated = yes owner = { has_variable = daoyu_all_owner_homeland } } } }
			daoyu_all_culture_effect = yes
			convert_population = { value = 1 target = scope:daoyu_target_religion }
		}
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_all_owner_homeland
	}
}

daoyu_change_variable = {
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_$VAR$ has_global_variable = daoyu_addvar } change_variable = { name = $VAR$ add = 100 } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_$VAR$ not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_addvar } } change_variable = { name = $VAR$ add = -100 } }
}
daoyu_a_o_r_homeland_effect = {
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_homeland } every_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_state } state_region = { remove_homeland = cu:$CULTURE$ } } }
	else = { every_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_state } state_region = { add_homeland = cu:$CULTURE$ } } }
}
daoyu_sort_by_chinese_or_english = {
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_sort_by_chinese } set_global_variable = daoyu_sort_C_$ALPHABET$ }
	else = { set_global_variable = daoyu_sort_E_$ALPHABET$ }
	trigger_event = { id = dcc.42 popup = yes }
}

daoyu_create_country = {
	capital = { save_scope_as = daoyu_capital }
	create_country = { tag = $TAG$ origin = this state = scope:daoyu_capital }
}
daoyu_set_pop_qualifications = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_all_owned_state }
		every_scope_state = { daoyu_detect_pop_qualifications = { PERCENT = $PERCENT$ } }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_incorporated_state }
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = { is_incorporated = yes }
			daoyu_detect_pop_qualifications = { PERCENT = $PERCENT$ }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_unincorporated_state }
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = { is_incorporated = no }
			daoyu_detect_pop_qualifications = { PERCENT = $PERCENT$ }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_target_state }
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state }
			daoyu_detect_pop_qualifications = { PERCENT = $PERCENT$ }
		}
	}
}
daoyu_detect_pop_qualifications = {
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_spq_machinists } daoyu_set_machinists_qualifications = { PERCENT = $PERCENT$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_spq_clergymen } daoyu_set_clergymen_qualifications = { PERCENT = $PERCENT$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_spq_shopkeepers } daoyu_set_shopkeepers_qualifications = { PERCENT = $PERCENT$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_spq_academics } daoyu_set_academics_qualifications = { PERCENT = $PERCENT$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_spq_officers } daoyu_set_officers_qualifications = { PERCENT = $PERCENT$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_spq_bureaucrats } daoyu_set_bureaucrats_qualifications = { PERCENT = $PERCENT$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_spq_engineers } daoyu_set_engineers_qualifications = { PERCENT = $PERCENT$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_spq_capitalists } daoyu_set_capitalists_qualifications = { PERCENT = $PERCENT$ } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_spq_aristocrats } daoyu_set_aristocrats_qualifications = { PERCENT = $PERCENT$ } }
}
daoyu_set_machinists_qualifications = {
	every_scope_pop = {
		limit = { not = { is_pop_type = machinists } strata = poor }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_qualifications_1 } set_pop_qualifications = { pop_type = machinists qualifications = $PERCENT$ } }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_qualifications_2 pop_has_primary_culture = yes } set_pop_qualifications = { pop_type = machinists qualifications = $PERCENT$ } }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_qualifications_3 pop_has_primary_culture = yes has_state_religion = yes } set_pop_qualifications = { pop_type = machinists qualifications = $PERCENT$ } }
	}
}
daoyu_set_clergymen_qualifications = {
	every_scope_pop = {
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_qualifications_1 strata = poor } set_pop_qualifications = { pop_type = clergymen qualifications = $PERCENT$ } }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_qualifications_2 strata = poor pop_has_primary_culture = yes } set_pop_qualifications = { pop_type = clergymen qualifications = $PERCENT$ } }

daoyu_mcomm = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital }
		if = { limit = { scope:daoyu_tst_2.state_region = s:$REGION$ } set_capital = $REGION$ }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_market }
		if = { limit = { scope:daoyu_tst_2.state_region = s:$REGION$ } set_market_capital = $REGION$ }
	}
}
daoyu_page_clean_effect = {
	remove_variable = daoyu_page_01
	remove_variable = daoyu_page_02
	remove_variable = daoyu_page_03
	remove_variable = daoyu_page_04
	remove_variable = daoyu_page_05
}

	remove_modifier = daoyu_power_bloc_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_power_bloc_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_power_bloc_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_power_bloc_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_power_bloc_modifier

daoyu_add_or_remove_principle = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_principle }
		power_bloc = {
			if = { limit = { has_principle = principle:principle_$PRI$_1 } remove_principle = principle_$PRI$_1 }
			if = { limit = { has_principle = principle:principle_$PRI$_2 } remove_principle = principle_$PRI$_2 }
			if = { limit = { has_principle = principle:principle_$PRI$_3 } remove_principle = principle_$PRI$_3 }
		}
	}
	else = { power_bloc = { add_principle = principle_$PRI$_3 } }
}
daoyu_upgrade_principle = {
	power_bloc = {
		if = {
			limit = { or = { has_principle = principle:principle_$PRI$_1 has_principle = principle:principle_$PRI$_2 } }
			remove_principle = principle_$PRI$_1 remove_principle = principle_$PRI$_2 add_principle = principle_$PRI$_3
		}
	}
}
